# <a name="required-diagnostic-data-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-103">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-103">Required diagnostic data for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-104">Informacije u ovom članku odnose se na verziju 1904 ili noviju verziju sljedećeg klijentskog softvera sustava Office instaliranog na računalu sa sustavom Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-105">Office 365 ProPlus i Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home ili druge verzije sustava Office koje su dio pretplate na Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-107">Project i Visio koji se isporučuju s nekim pretplatničkim tarifama, kao što su Project Online Professional ili Visio Online Plan 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-108">Dijagnostički podaci koriste se da bi Office uvijek bio siguran i ažuran, kao i radi otkrivanja, dijagnosticiranja i rješavanja problema te poboljšavanja proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-108">Diagnostic data is used to keep Office secure and up-to-date, detect, diagnose and fix problems, and also make product improvements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-109">Ti podaci ne sadrže korisnikovo ime ili adresu e-pošte, sadržaj korisnikovih datoteka ni informacije o aplikacijama koje nisu povezane sa sustavom Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-109">This data does not include a user’s name or email address, the content of the user’s files, or information about apps unrelated to Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-110">To su dijagnostički podaci o klijentskom softveru sustava Office koji se koristi na računalima sa sustavom Windows, a koji se prikupljaju i šalju Microsoftu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-110">This diagnostic data is collected and sent to Microsoft about Office client software being used on computers running Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-111">Neki su dijagnostički podaci obavezni, a neki nisu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-111">Some diagnostic data is required, while some diagnostic data is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-112">Omogućujemo vam da odaberete hoćete li nam slati obavezne ili dijagnostičke podatke putem kontrola zaštite privatnosti, kao što su postavke pravilnika za tvrtke i ustanove.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-112">We give you the ability to choose whether to send us required or optional diagnostic data through the use of privacy controls, such as policy settings for organizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-113">Dijagnostičke podatke koji nam se šalju možete pogledati pomoću preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-113">You can see the diagnostic data being sent to us by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-114">***Obavezni dijagnostički podaci*** minimalni su podaci potrebni da bi Office bio siguran i ažuran te da bi na uređaju na kojem je instaliran funkcionirao na očekivan način.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-114">***Required diagnostic data*** is the minimum data necessary to help keep Office secure, up-to-date, and performing as expected on the device it’s installed on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-115">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci omogućuju da otkrijete probleme sa sustavom Office koji mogu biti povezani s konfiguracijom uređaja ili softvera.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-115">Required diagnostic data helps to identify problems with Office that may be related to a device or software configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-116">Na primjer, pomoću njih možete utvrditi ruši li se značajka sustava Office češće u određenoj verziji operacijskog sustava, zbog tek uvedenih značajki ili kada se onemoguće određene značajke sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-116">For example, it can help determine if an Office feature crashes more frequently on a particular operating system version, with newly introduced features, or when certain Office features are disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-117">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci omogućuju nam da otkrijemo, dijagnosticiramo i brže riješimo te probleme kako bi se smanjio utjecaj na korisnike ili tvrtke i ustanove.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-117">Required diagnostic data helps us detect, diagnose, and fix these problems more quickly so the impact to users or organizations is reduced.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-118">Dodatne informacije o dijagnostičkim podacima potražite u ovim člancima:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-118">For more information about diagnostic data, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-119">Neobavezni dijagnostički podaci za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-119">Optional diagnostic data for Office</span></span>](optional-diagnostic-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-120">Korištenje preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka sa sustavom Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-120">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-121">Ako ste administrator za tvrtku ili ustanovu, možda će vas zanimati i sljedeći članci:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-121">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-122">Pregled kontrola za zaštitu privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-122">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-123">Korištenje postavki pravilnika za upravljanje kontrolama za zaštitu privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-123">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="categories-data-subtypes-events-and-data-fields-for-required-diagnostic-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-124">Kategorije, podvrste podataka, događaji i podatkovna polja za obavezne dijagnostičke podatke</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-124">Categories, data subtypes, events, and data fields for required diagnostic data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-125">Obavezni dijagnostički podaci organizirani su u kategorije i podvrste podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-125">Required diagnostic data is organized into categories and data subtypes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-126">U svakoj su podvrsti podataka događaji koji sadrže podatkovna polja specifična tom događaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-126">Within each data subtype are events, which contain data fields that are specific to that event.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-127">U sljedećoj su tablici navedene kategorije za obavezne dijagnostičke podatke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-127">The following table provides a list of the categories for required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-128">Navedene su podvrste podataka u svakoj kategoriji i opis fokusa za tu podvrstu podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-128">The data subtypes within each category are listed, along with a description of the focus for that data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-129">Prikazat će se veze na odgovarajući odjeljak podvrste podataka u kojem ćete naći sljedeće informacije:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-129">There are links to each data subtype section where you’ll find the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="65b74-130">popis događaja u toj podvrsti podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-130">A list of events in that data subtype</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="65b74-131">opis svakog događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-131">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="65b74-132">popis podatkovnih polja u svakom događaju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-132">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="65b74-133">opis svakog podatkovnog polja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-133">A description of each data field</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-134">**Kategorija**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-134">**Category**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-135">**Podvrsta podataka**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-135">**Data subtype**</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-136">**Opis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-136">**Description**</span></span>    |
| ---------- | ------------- | ---- |
| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-137">**Instalacija softvera i instalirani softver**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-137">**Software setup and inventory**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-138">Instalacija sustava Office i instalirani softver</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-138">Office setup and inventory</span></span>](#office-setup-and-inventory-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-139">Instalirani proizvod, njegova verzija i njegov status instalacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-139">Installed product and version and the installation status.</span></span>  |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-140">Konfiguracija dodatka za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-140">Office add-in configuration</span></span>](#office-add-in-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-141">Softverski dodaci i njihove postavke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-141">Software add-ins and their settings.</span></span>     |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-142">Sigurnost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-142">Security</span></span>](#security-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-143">Uvjeti za pogreške u dokumentima, značajkama i dodacima koji mogu ugroziti sigurnost, uključujući spremnost proizvoda za ažuriranje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-143">Document, feature, and add-in error conditions that may compromise security, including product update readiness.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-144">**Korištenje proizvoda i usluga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-144">**Product and service usage**</span></span>    | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-145">Uspjeh značajki aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-145">Application feature success</span></span>](#application-feature-success-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-146">Uspješno funkcioniranje aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-146">Success of application functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-147">Ograničeno na otvaranje i zatvaranje aplikacije i dokumenata, uređivanje datoteka i zajedničko korištenje dokumenata (suradnju).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-147">Limited to opening and closing of the application and documents, file editing, and file sharing (collaboration).</span></span> |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-148">Status i pokretanje aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-148">Application status and boot</span></span>](#application-status-and-boot-subtype)    | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-149">Utvrđivanje je li došlo do određenih događaja povezanih sa značajkama, kao što je pokretanje ili zaustavljanje, te utvrđivanje je li značajka pokrenuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-149">Determination if specific feature events have occurred, such as start or stop, and if feature is running.</span></span>   |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-150">Konfiguracija pristupačnosti za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-150">Office accessibility configuration</span></span>](#office-accessibility-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-151">Značajke pristupačnosti u sustavu Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-151">Office accessibility features</span></span>       |
| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-152">**Performanse proizvoda i usluga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-152">**Product and service performance**</span></span>       | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-153">Neočekivano zatvaranje aplikacije (rušenje)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-153">Unexpected application exit (crash)</span></span>](#unexpected-application-exit-crash-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-154">Neočekivana zatvaranja aplikacija i stanje aplikacije kada se to dogodi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-154">Unexpected application exits and the state of the application when that happens.</span></span>    |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-155">Performanse značajki aplikacije </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-155">Application feature performance </span></span>](#application-feature-performance-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-156">Loše vrijeme odziva ili performanse u situacijama kao što su pokretanje aplikacije ili otvaranje datoteke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-156">Poor response time or performance for scenarios such as application start up or opening a file.</span></span> |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-157">Pogreška aktivnosti aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-157">Application activity error</span></span>](#application-activity-error-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-158">Pogreške u funkcioniranju značajke ili korisničkog okruženja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-158">Errors in functionality of a feature or user experience.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="65b74-159">**Povezivost i konfiguracija uređaja**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-159">**Device connectivity and configuration**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-160">Povezivost i konfiguracija uređaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-160">Device connectivity and configuration</span></span>](#device-connectivity-and-configuration-subtype) | <span data-ttu-id="65b74-161">Stanje mrežne veze i postavke uređaja, kao što je memorija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-161">Network connection state and device settings, such as memory.</span></span> |


> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-162">Kategorije su prikazane u pregledniku dijagnostičkih podataka, ali podvrste podataka nisu prikazane.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-162">Categories are shown in the Diagnostic Data Viewer, but data subtypes are not shown.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-163">Podatkovno polje označeno kao *Zastarjelo* uklonjeno je ili će uskoro biti uklonjeno iz obaveznih dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-163">A data field marked *Obsolete* has been or will soon be removed from required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-164">Neka od tih podatkovnih polja su duplikati koji su nastali prilikom moderniziranja dijagnostičkih podataka i korišteni su da bi se spriječio prekid aktivnih izvješća dijagnostičkog nadzora.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-164">Some of these data fields are duplicates that arose as diagnostic data was modernized and were used to ensure no service disruption to live diagnostic monitoring reports.</span></span>

## <a name="categories-and-data-fields-that-are-common-for-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-165">Kategorije i podatkovna polja koja su zajednička svim događajima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-165">Categories and data fields that are common for all events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-166">Ovdje su i neke informacije koje se odnose na sve događaje, bez obzira na kategoriju ili podvrstu podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-166">There is some information about events that is common to all events, regardless of category or data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-167">Te opće informacije, koje se ponekad nazivaju *podatkovni ugovori*, organizirane su po kategorijama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-167">This common information, which is sometimes referred to as *data contracts*, is organized into categories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-168">Svaka kategorija sadrži polja, a ta su polja metapodaci i svojstva pojedinog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-168">Each category contains fields, and these fields are the metadata and properties of an individual event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-169">Te podatke možete pogledati pomoću preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-169">You can view this information by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-170">Kategorije podataka koji se prikupljaju o događajima mogu se podijeliti u dvije grupe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-170">The categories of information that is collected about events can be divided into two groups:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-171">Informacije zajedničke svim događajima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-171">Information common to all events</span></span>](#information-common-to-all-events)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-172">Informacije koje izričito podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-172">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection</span></span>](#information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection)

### <a name="information-common-to-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-173">*Informacije zajedničke svim događajima*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-173">*Information common to all events*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-174">U sljedeće kategorije prikupljaju se informacije zajedničke svim događajima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-174">Information common to all events is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="app"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-175">Aplikacija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-175">App</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-176">Informacije o aplikaciji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-176">Information about the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-177">Sva su polja konstante za sve sesije određene verzije navedene aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-177">All fields are constant for all sessions of a given application version.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-178">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-178">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-179">**Grana** ― grana iz koje dolazi navedena međuverzija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-179">**Branch** - The branch that the given build came from.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-180">Omogućuje da utvrdimo iz koje vrste grane dolazi navedena međuverzija kako bismo ispravno usmjerili rješenja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-180">Allows us to determine what type of branch a given build came from so that we can correctly target fixes.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-181">**InstallType** ― identifikator koji određuje način na koji je korisnik instalirao aplikaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-181">**InstallType** - An enumerator that identifies how the user installed the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-182">Omogućuje da utvrdimo stvaraju li mehanizmi određene instalacije probleme kojih nema u mehanizmima drugih instalacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-182">Allows us to determine if specific install mechanisms are creating issues that are not seen in other installation mechanisms.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-183">**Naziv** ― naziv aplikacije koja daje podatke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-183">**Name** - The name of the application that is providing the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-184">Omogućuje prepoznavanje aplikacije s kojom se pojavljuje problem kako bismo ga znali riješiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-184">Allows us to identify which application is showing an issue so we know how to address it.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-185">**Platforma** ― općenita klasifikacija platforme na kojoj je pokrenuta aplikacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-185">**Platform** - The broad classification of the platform on which the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-186">Omogućuje da odredimo na kojim se platformama problem pojavljuje kako bismo mogli ispravno odrediti njegov prioritet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-186">Allows us to identify on which platforms an issue may be occurring so that we can correctly prioritize the issue.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-187">**Verzija** ― verzija aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-187">**Version** - The version of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-188">Omogućuje prepoznavanje verzija proizvoda s kojima se pojavljuje problem kako bismo mogli ispravno odrediti njegov prioritet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-188">Allows us to identify which versions of the product are showing an issue so that we can correctly prioritize it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-190">Identifikator povezan s instancom sustava Office na uređaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-190">Identifier related to an Office instance on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-191">Konstanta za sve sesije svih aplikacija određene verzije instalacije za pakete s više aplikacija ili konstanta za sve sesije određene verzije aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-191">Constant for all sessions of all apps of a given installation version for multi-app suites, or constant for all sessions of a given application version.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-200">**DiagnosticConsentLevel** – označava razinu pristanka za dijagnostičke podatke koju je korisnik dao</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-200">**DiagnosticConsentLevel** – Indicates what level of diagnostic data consent the user has given</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-206">**ControllerConnectedServicesState** – označava ima li korisnik pristup neobaveznim povezanim iskustvima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-206">**ControllerConnectedServicesState** – Indicates whether the user has access to optional connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-207">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateSourceLocation** – označava kako je napravljen korisnikov odabir za neobavezna povezana iskustva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-207">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user’s choice for optional connected experiences was made</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-212">**DownloadContentState** – označava je li korisnik odlučio omogućiti ili onemogućiti povezana iskustva koja preuzimaju internetski sadržaj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-212">**DownloadContentState** – Indicates whether the user has chosen to enable or disable connected experiences that download online content</span></span>

#### <a name="release"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-229">Izdanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-229">Release</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-230">Podaci koji se odnose na kanal izdavanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-230">Information related to the release channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-231">Sva su polja konstante za sve sesije svih aplikacija određene verzije instalacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-231">All fields are constant for all sessions of all apps of a given installation version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-232">Određuje grupu uređaja u jednoj fazi ciklusa izdavanja proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-232">Identifies a group of devices all in one phase of a product release cycle.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-233">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-233">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-236">**AudienceGroup** – označava krug iz kojeg potječu podaci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-236">**AudienceGroup** - Identifies the ring where data is coming from.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-237">Omogućuje postupno uvođenje značajki i prepoznavanje potencijalnih problema prije nego što dođu do većine korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-237">Allows us to roll out features in a staged fashion and identify potential issues before they reach most users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-238">**Kanal** – kanal putem kojeg se izdaje proizvod.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-238">**Channel** - The channel that the product is being released through.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-239">Omogućuje da odredimo utječe li problem na jedan od naših kanala za uvođenje drugačije od drugih.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-239">Allows us to identify if an issue is impacting one of our rollout channels differently than others.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-240">**Međuverzija** – određuje međuverziju proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-240">**Fork** - Identifies the fork of the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-241">Omogućuje mehanizam za prikupljanje podataka u skupu brojeva međuverzija radi prepoznavanja problema povezanih s određenim izdanjem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-241">Allows a mechanism to aggregate data across a set of build numbers to identify issues related to a given release.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-242">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-242">Session</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-243">Informacije o sesiji postupka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-243">Information about the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-244">Sva su polja konstante za ovu sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-244">All fields are constant for this session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-245">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-245">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-246">**ABConfigs** – označava skup međuverzija koje se izvode u određenoj sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-246">**ABConfigs** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-247">Omogućuje prepoznavanje pojedinačnih međuverzija koje se izvode u sesiji kako bismo utvrdili je li međuverzija izvor problema koji utječe na korisnike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-247">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-248">**EcsETag** – pokazatelj iz sustava međuverzija koji predstavlja međuverzije poslane na računalo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-248">**EcsETag** - An indicator from the flighting system that represents the flights sent to the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-249">Omogućuje prepoznavanje međuverzija koje utječu na određenu sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-249">Allows us to identify what flights might be impacting a given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-250">**Zastavice** – zastavice za praćenje bit-maske koje se odnose na cijelu sesiju, trenutno se uglavnom odnosi na uzorkovanje i mogućnosti dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-250">**Flags** - Bitmask tracking flags applicable to an entire session, currently primarily focused on sampling and diagnostic data options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-251">Omogućuje kontrolu ponašanja određene sesije u odnosu prema dijagnostičkim podacima koje sesija generira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-251">Allows us to control how a given session behaves in relation to the diagnostic data that the session generates.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-252">**ID** – jedinstveno označava određenu sesiju podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-252">**Id** - Uniquely identifies a given session of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-253">Omogućuje utvrđivanje utjecaja problema procjenom broja zahvaćenih sesija te postoje li zajedničke značajke tih sesija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-253">Allows us to identify the impact of issues by evaluating the number of sessions that are impacted and if there are common features of those sessions.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-254">**ImpressionId** – označava skup međuverzija koje se izvode u određenoj sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-254">**ImpressionId** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-255">Omogućuje prepoznavanje pojedinačnih međuverzija koje se izvode u sesiji kako bismo utvrdili je li međuverzija izvor problema koji utječe na korisnike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-255">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-256">**MeasuresEnabled** – zastavica koja označava jesu li podaci trenutne sesije uzorkovani.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-256">**MeasuresEnabled** - Flag indicating if the current sessions data is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-257">Omogućuje da utvrdimo kako statistički procijeniti podatke prikupljene iz određene sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-257">Allows us to determine how to statistically evaluate the data that is gathered from the given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-258">**SamplingClientId** – ID klijenta kojim se utvrđuje je li dio uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-258">**SamplingClientId** - The id of the client used to determine if it is part of sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-259">Omogućuje da utvrdimo zašto je pojedinačna sesija uključena ili isključena iz uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-259">Allows us to determine why an individual session was included or excluded from sampling.</span></span>

#### <a name="user"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-260">Korisnik</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-260">User</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-261">Pruža informacije o klijentu za SKU-ove komercijalnog softvera.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-261">Provides tenant information for commercial software SKUs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-262">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-262">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-263">**PrimaryIdentityHash** – identifikator u obliku pseudonima koji predstavlja trenutnog korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-263">**PrimaryIdentityHash** – A pseudonymous identifier that represents the current user.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-264">**PrimaryIdentitySpace** – vrsta identiteta sadržana u identifikatoru PrimaryIdentityHash.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-264">**PrimaryIdentitySpace** – The type of identity contained in the PrimaryIdentityHash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-265">MASCID, OrgIdCID ili UserObjectId.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-265">One of MASCID, OrgIdCID or UserObjectId.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-266">**TenantGroup** – vrsta klijenta kojem pripada pretplata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-266">**TenantGroup** - The type of the tenant that the subscription belongs to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-267">Omogućuje klasifikaciju problema i utvrđivanje je li problem rasprostranjen ili ograničen na skup korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-267">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-268">**TenantId** – klijent s kojim je povezana pretplata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-268">**TenantId** - The tenant that a user’s subscription is tied to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-269">Omogućuje klasifikaciju problema i utvrđivanje je li problem rasprostranjen ili ograničen na skup korisnika ili određenog klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-269">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users or a specific tenant.</span></span>

### <a name="information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-270">*Informacije koje izričito podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-270">*Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-271">Informacije koje izričito podržavaju prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka prikupljaju se u sljedećim kategorijama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-271">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="activity"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-272">Aktivnost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-272">Activity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-273">Informacije za shvaćanje uspješnosti samog događaja prikupljanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-273">Information to understand the success of the collection event itself.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-274">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-274">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-275">**AggMode** – govori sustavu kako prikupiti rezultate aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-275">**AggMode** - Tells the system how to aggregate activity results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-276">Omogućuje da smanjimo količinu podataka prenesenih s korisnikovog računala prikupljanjem rezultata aktivnosti u jedan događaj koji se šalje povremeno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-276">Allows us to reduce the amount of information uploaded from a user’s machine by aggregating activity results into a single event that gets sent periodically.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-277">**Count** – broj izvršavanja aktivnosti ako je broj iz skupnog događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-277">**Count** - The number of times the activity happened if the count is from an aggregated event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-278">Omogućuje da odredimo koliko je često aktivnost uspjela na temelju načina prikupljanja aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-278">Allows us to determine how often an activity succeeded or failed based on the aggregation mode of the activity.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-279">**CV** – vrijednost koja određuje odnos između aktivnosti i segmenata aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-279">**CV** - A value that identifies the relationship between activities and sub-activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-280">Omogućuje ponovno stvaranje odnosa između ugniježđenih aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-280">Allows us to rebuild the relationship between nested activities.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-281">**Trajanje** – vrijeme potrebno za izvršavanje aktivnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-281">**Duration** - The length of time the activity took to execute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-282">Omogućuje prepoznavanje problema s performansama koji negativno utječu na korisničko okruženje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-282">Allows us to identify performance issues that are negatively impacting the users experience.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-283">**Rezultat**.\*\* Kod\*\* – kod koji je definirala aplikacija za prepoznavanje određenih rezultata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-283">**Result**.**Code** - An application defined code to identify a given results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-284">Omogućuje da utvrdimo specifične pojedinosti o određenoj pogrešci, primjerice kod pogreške koji može se koristiti za klasifikaciju i rješavanje problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-284">Allows us to determine more specific details of a given failure such as a failure code that can be used to classify and fix issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-285">**Result.Tag** – oznaka cijelog broja koja označava mjesto u kodu u kojem je generiran rezultat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-285">**Result.Tag** - An integer tag that identifies the location in code where the result was generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-286">Omogućuje jasno utvrđivanje mjesta u kodu na kojem je rezultat generiran što omogućuje klasifikaciju pogrešaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-286">Allows us to distinctly identify the location in code where a result was generated which enables classification of failures.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-287">**Rezultat**.**Vrsta** – vrsta koda rezultata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-287">**Result**.**Type** - The type of the result code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-288">Određuje vrstu poslanog koda rezultata kako bi se vrijednost ispravno tumačila.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-288">Identifies what type of result code was sent so that the value can be correctly interpreted.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-289">**Uspjeh** – zastavica koja označava je li aktivnost uspjela.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-289">**Success** - A flag indicating if the activity succeeded or failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-290">Omogućuje da utvrdimo uspijevaju li radnje koje korisnik izvršava u proizvodu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-290">Allows us to determine if actions the user takes in the product are succeeding or failing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-291">Time se omogućuje prepoznavanje problema koji utječu na korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-291">This allows us to identify issues that are impacting the user.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-292">Aplikacija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-292">Application</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-293">Informacije o instalaciji aplikacije iz koje se prikupljaju događaji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-293">Information about the installation of the application from which the events are being gathered.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-294">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-294">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-295">**Arhitektura** – arhitektura aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-295">**Architecture** - The architecture of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-296">Omogućuje nam da klasificiramo pogreške koje mogu biti specifične za arhitekturu aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-296">Let’s us classify errors that might be specific to an architecture of the application.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-297">**Click2RunPackageVersion** – broj verzije paketa Klikom do cilja koji je instalirao aplikaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-297">**Click2RunPackageVersion** - The version number of the Click-To-Run package that installed the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-298">Omogućuje da utvrdimo verziju instalacijskog programa korištenu za instalaciju sustava Office kako bismo prepoznali probleme vezane uz postavljanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-298">Allows us to identify which version of the installer was used to install Office so we can identify setup related issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-299">**DistributionChannel** – kanal u kojem je aplikacija implementirana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-299">**DistributionChannel** - The channel where the app was deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-300">Omogućuje da podijelimo dolazne podatke kako bismo utvrdili utječu li problemi na ciljne skupine.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-300">Allows us to partition incoming data so we can determine if issues are impacting audiences.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-301">**InstallMethod** – određuje je li sustav nadograđen na trenutnu međuverziju sustava Office sa starije međuverzije, vraćen na nju ili je u pitanju nova instalacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-301">**InstallMethod** - Whether the current build of Office was upgraded from an older build, rolled back to an older build, or a fresh install.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-302">**IsClickToRunInstall** – zastavica koja označava radi li se o instalaciji „klikom do cilja“.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-302">**IsClickToRunInstall** - Flag indicating if install was a click to run install.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-303">Omogućuje da prepoznamo probleme koji mogu biti specifični za mehanizam instalacije Klikom do cilja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-303">Allows us to identify issues that might be specific to the Click-To-Run install mechanism.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-304">**IsDebug** – zastavica koja označava radi li se o međuverziji sustava Office za ispravljanje pogrešaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-304">**IsDebug** - Flag indicating if the office build is a Debug build.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-305">Omogućuje da utvrdimo potječu li problemi iz međuverzija za ispravljanje pogrešaka koje se ponašaju drugačije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-305">Allows us to identify if issues are coming from Debug builds which may behave differently .</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-306">**IsInstalledOnExternalStorage** – zastavica koja označava je li Office instaliran na vanjskom uređaju za pohranu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-306">**IsInstalledOnExternalStorage** - Flag indicating if Office was installed on an external storage device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-307">Omogućuje nam da odredimo mogu li se problemi povezati s mjestom za vanjsku pohranu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-307">Let’s us determine if issues can be traced to an external storage location.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-308">**IsOEMInstalled** – zastavica koja označava je li Office instalirao proizvođač originalne opreme (OEM).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-308">**IsOEMInstalled** - Flag indicating if Office was installed by an original equipment manufacturer (OEM).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-309">Omogućuje nam da odredimo je li aplikaciju instalirao OEM, što nam može olakšati klasifikaciju i prepoznavanje problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-309">Let’s us determine if the application was installed by an OEM which can help us classify and identify issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-310">**PreviousVersion** – verzija sustava Office koja je već instalirana na računalu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-310">**PreviousVersion** - The version of Office that was previously installed on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-311">Omogućuje da se vratimo na prethodnu verziju ako postoji problem s trenutnom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-311">Allows us to roll back to a previous version if the current one has an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-312">**ProcessFileName** – naziv datoteke aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-312">**ProcessFileName** - The name of the application filename.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-313">Omogućuje prepoznavanje naziva izvršne datoteke koja generira podatke jer može postojati nekoliko različitih naziva datoteka procesa koji izvještavaju s istim nazivom aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-313">Allows us to identify the name of the executable which is generating the data as there may be several different process filenames reporting as the same app name.</span></span>

#### <a name="event"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-370">Događaj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-370">Event</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-371">Informacije specifične za događaj, uključujući njegov jedinstveni identifikator u sesiji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-371">Event-specific information, including its unique identifier in the session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-372">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-372">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-373">**Ugovor** – popis svih ugovora koje događaj implementira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-373">**Contract** - A list of any contracts that the event is implementing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-374">Omogućuje da procijenimo koji su podaci dio pojedinačnog događaja kako bismo ih mogli učinkovito obraditi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-374">Allows us to evaluate what data is part of the individual event so that we can process it effectively.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-375">**CV** – vrijednost koja omogućuje prepoznavanje povezanih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-375">**CV** - A value that allows us to identify events that are related to one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-376">Koristi se za dijagnostiku kako bismo prepoznali uzorke povezanog ponašanja ili povezanih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-376">Used for diagnostics to allow us to identify patterns of related behavior or related events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-377">**Zastavice** – informacije koje se koriste za promjenu načina na koji događaj odgovara.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-377">**Flags** - Information used to alter how a given event responds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-378">Koristi se za upravljanje načinom na koji se događaj tretira radi prijenosa podataka Microsoftu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-378">Used to manage how a given event is treated for the purposes of uploading the data to Microsoft.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-379">**Id** – jedinstveni identifikator za događaj.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-379">**Id** - A unique identifier for the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-380">Omogućuje jedinstveno identificiranje primljenih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-380">Allows us to uniquely identify the events that are being received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-381">**Naziv** – naziv događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-381">**Name** - The name of the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-382">Omogućuje prepoznavanje događaja koji šalje klijent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-382">Allows to identify the event that was being sent from the client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-383">**Pravilo** – identifikator pravila koje je generiralo podatke ako ih je generiralo pravilo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-383">**Rule** - An identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-384">Omogućuje prepoznavanje izvora dijela podataka tako da možemo provjeriti parametre tog događaja i njima upravljati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-384">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-385">**RuleId** – identifikator pravila koje je generiralo podatke ako ih je generiralo pravilo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-385">**RuleId** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-386">Omogućuje prepoznavanje izvora dijela podataka tako da možemo provjeriti parametre tog događaja i njima upravljati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-386">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-389">**RuleVersion** – identifikator pravila koje je generiralo podatke ako ih je generiralo pravilo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-389">**RuleVersion** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-390">Omogućuje prepoznavanje izvora dijela podataka tako da možemo provjeriti parametre tog događaja i njima upravljati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-390">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-391">**SampleRate** – oznaka postotka korisnika koji šalju taj dio podataka. Time se omogućuje statistička analiza podataka i veoma česte točke podataka ne zahtijevaju da to šalju svi korisnici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-391">**SampleRate** - An indication of what percentage of users are sending this piece of data This allows us to do statistical analysis of the data and for very common data points not require that to be sent by all users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-392">**SchemaVersion** – verzija sheme koja se koristi za generiranje dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-392">**SchemaVersion** - The version of the schema used to generate diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-393">Obavezno za upravljanje podacima koje šalje klijent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-393">Required to manage data being sent form the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-394">Time se omogućuju promjene podataka koje šalje svaki klijent tijekom vremena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-394">This allows changes over time in what data is being sent from each client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-395">**Slijed** – brojač koji navodi redoslijed kojim je događaj generiran na klijentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-395">**Sequence** - A counter that identifies the order that an event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-396">Omogućuje numeriranje primljenih podataka kako bismo prepoznali korake koji su doveli do problema koji utječe na klijente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-396">Allows the data being received to be ordered so that we can identify what steps may have led to an issue that is impacting clients.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-397">**Izvor** – izvorni kanal upotrijebljen za prijenos podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-397">**Source** - The source pipeline that was used to upload the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-398">Obavezno za praćenje svih kanala za prijenos radi ukupnog stanja i prepoznavanja problema s kanalom za prijenos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-398">Required to monitor each of our upload pipelines for overall health and to help identify issues with the upload pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-399">Time se omogućuje praćenje pojedinačnih kanala za prijenos kako bi bili usklađeni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-399">This allows us to monitor individual upload pipelines to make sure they remain compliant.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-400">**Vrijeme** – vrijeme generiranja događaja na klijentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-400">**Time** - The time that the event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-401">Omogućuje sinkroniziranje i provjeru valjanosti redoslijeda događaja generiranih na klijentu kao i uspostavu parametara za mjerenje performansi za korisničke upute.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-401">Allows us to synchronize and validate the order of events generated on the client as well as establish performance metrics for user instructions.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-419">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-419">Session</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-420">Informacije o sesiji postupka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-420">Information about the process session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-421">Ova kategorija sadrži sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-421">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-422">**ABConfigsDelta** – prati razliku između aktualnih podataka ABConfigs i prethodne vrijednosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-422">**ABConfigsDelta** - Tracks the difference between the current ABConfigs data and the previous value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-423">Omogućuje praćenje novih međuverzija na računalu da bismo lakše otkrili je li nova međuverzija odgovorna za problem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-423">Allows us to track what new flights are on the machine to help identify if a new flight is responsible for an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-424">**CollectibleClassification** – klase informacija koje sesija može prikupiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-424">**CollectibleClassification** - The classes of information the session can collect.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-425">Omogućuje filtriranje sesija na temelju podataka koje imaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-425">Allows filtering of sessions based on the data they would have.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-426">**DisableTelemetry** – zastavica koja označava je li ključ DisableTelemetry postavljen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-426">**DisableTelemetry** - Flag indicating if the DisableTelemetry key is set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-427">Omogućuje da utvrdimo je li sesija izvješćivala dijagnostičke podatke koji nisu EssentialServiceMetadata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-427">Allows us to know if a session was not reporting diagnostic data other than EssentialServiceMetadata.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-428">**SamplingKey** – ključ koji određuje je li sesija uzorkovana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-428">**SamplingKey** - The key used to determine whether the session is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-429">Omogućuje da utvrdimo kako pojedine sesije odlučuju hoće li biti uzorkovane.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-429">Allows us to understand how individual sessions are making their choice of whether they are sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-430">**SamplingMethod** – metoda koja se koristi za utvrđivanje pravila uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-430">**SamplingMethod** - The method used to determine sampling policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-431">Omogućuje da utvrdimo koji podaci dolaze iz sesije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-431">Allows us to understand what data is coming from a session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-432">**Slijed** – jedinstveni numerički identifikator za sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-432">**Sequence** - A unique numeric identifier for the session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-433">Omogućuje određivanje redoslijeda sesija za analizu problema koji su se pojavili.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-433">Allows the ordering of sessions for analysis of then issues might have occurred.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-434">**Pokretanje** – vrijeme pokretanja sesije postupka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-434">**Start** - The boot time of the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-435">Omogućuje da utvrdimo kada je sesija pokrenuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-435">Allows us to establish when the session started.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-436">**TimeZoneBiasInMinutes** – razlika u minutama između UTC-a i lokalnog vremena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-436">**TimeZoneBiasInMinutes** - The difference in minutes between UTC and the local time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-437">Omogućuje normalizaciju UTC-a na lokalno vrijeme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-437">Allows normalization of UTC times back to the local time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-438">**SamplingClientIdValue** – vrijednost ključa za određivanje uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-438">**SamplingClientIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-439">Omogućuje da utvrdimo zašto je sesija uzorkovana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-439">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-440">**SamplingDeviceIdValue** – vrijednost ključa za određivanje uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-440">**SamplingDeviceIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-441">Omogućuje da utvrdimo zašto je sesija uzorkovana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-441">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-442">**SamplingSessionKValue** – napredni metapodaci uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-442">**SamplingSessionKValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-443">Koristi se za procjenu statističkog značenja primljenih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-443">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-444">**SamplingSessionNValue** – napredni metapodaci uzorkovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-444">**SamplingSessionNValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-445">Koristi se za procjenu statističkog značenja primljenih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-445">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

#### <a name="officetargetedmessagingensurecached"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-493">Prati je li preuzet paket za dinamičko radno područje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-493">Tracks if a package for Dynamic Canvas was downloaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-494">Smatra se softverskom konfiguracijom jer se paket mora uspješno preuzeti da bi klijent mogao omogućiti pravo iskustvo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-494">Considered a software configuration because the package must be successfully downloaded to enable the client to render the right experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-495">Osobito je važno u korisničkim pretplatama u kojima obavještavamo korisnika putem radnog područja da je licenca istekla.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-495">Is especially critical in consumer subscriptions where we use canvas to communicate to the user that the license has expired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-496">Koristi se za praćenje metapodataka paketa dinamičnog sadržaja kojeg je preuzeo i predmemorirao proizvod, kao i rezultate radnji izvršenih na paketu: neuspjela preuzimanja, neuspjela raspakiranja, pogreške provjere dosljednosti, pronalaženje objekata u predmemoriji, načini korištenja paketa, izvori preuzimanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-496">Used to track metadata of a dynamic content package downloaded and cached by the product as well as results of operations performed on the package: download failures, unpacking failures, consistency checks failures, cache hits, package usages, download sources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-497">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-497">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated –** Booleova zastavica koja označava je li uspjelo stvaranje mape predmemorije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated -** Boolean flag indicating if cache folder creation succeed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-499">**Data\_CdnPath – izvorna adresa paketa-**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-499">**Data\_CdnPath – source address of the package-**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-500">**Data\_EnsureCached –** Booleova zastavica koja označava je li paket sadržaja predmemoriran</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-500">**Data\_EnsureCached -** Boolean flag indicating if content package was cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder –** problemi s lokalnim diskom uzrokuju pogreške tijekom stvaranja direktorija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder -** local disk issues causing failure in directory creation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed –** zastavica koja označava je li paket preuzet, ali ga klijent ne može čitati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed -** flag indicating if package was downloaded, but the client can’t read it</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess –** nema problema s diskom ni problema s konfiguracijom koji ne dopuštaju čitanje tijeka podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess -** no disk issues nor configuration issues which doesn’t let the file stream to be read</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess –** statusi pokušaja raspakiranja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess -** unpacking attempts statuses</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-519">**Data\_SuccessSource –** površina za koju je paket preuzet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-519">**Data\_SuccessSource -** surface for which the package was downloaded</span></span>

#### <a name="officevisiovisiosku"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-520">Office.Visio.VisioSKU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-520">Office.Visio.VisioSKU</span></span>

### <a name="office-add-in-configuration-subtype"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-525">*Podvrsta konfiguracije dodatka za Office*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-525">*Office add-in configuration subtype*</span></span>

data-ttu-id="65b74-548"> ExchangeGetEntitlements (i ExchangeGetManifests) mogu se također pozvati na zahtjev kada je glavna aplikacija pokrenuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-548"> ExchangeGetEntitlements (and ExchangeGetManifests) could also be called on demand after host application has been running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-549"> Svrha je toga da se ne učita veliki DLL ako nije potreban.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-549"> The idea is to not load the large DLL if we don’t need to.</span></span> <span #### <a name="officefileiocsiccachedfilecsisavefilebasic"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-934">Omogućuje da utvrdimo je li datoteka uspješno spremljena u FIO sloju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-934">Allows us to know if a file was successfully saved from the FIO Layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-935">Koristi se za stanje i nadzor značajke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-935">Used for Feature Health and monitoring.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-936">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-936">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-937">**Activity.Group –** oznaka koja omogućuje postavljanje grupiranja događaja nadzora za upravljanje ukupnim uspjehom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-937">**Activity.Group -** tag that allows a set of monitoring events to be grouped to manage overall success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-938">**Activity.IsHVA –** zastavica koja označava da je događaj ključan za uspjeh korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-938">**Activity.IsHVA -** flag to indicate that event is critical to user success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-939">**Data.AsyncOpen –** zastavica koja označava da je dokument otvoren sa sadržajem koji je primljen nakon otvaranja glavnog tijela</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-939">**Data.AsyncOpen -** flag to indicate that the document was opened with content that arrived after the main body was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered –** promjena dijagnostike praćenja koja označava da je zatražena osnovna verzija dokumenta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered -** Change tracking diagnostic indicating that the base version of the document was requested</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationnewdocument"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1214">Prikuplja se kada PowerPoint stvori novu prezentaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1214">Collected when PowerPoint creates a new presentation.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1215"> Obuhvaća metriku uspjeha, neuspjeha i performansi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1215"> Includes success failure and performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1216">Te se informacije koriste da bismo uspješno stvorili datoteke bez smanjenih performansi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1216">This information is used to ensure we can create files successfully and with no degradation in performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1217">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1217">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1219">**FLifeguarded** – je li zaštićen životni vijek dokumenta (značajka koja vraća stanje oštećenog dokumenta bez slanja upita korisniku)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1219">**FLifeguarded** – Is document life guarded (feature that restores corrupt document state without prompting user)</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsave"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1280">Prikuplja se svaki put kada PowerPoint izvodi spremanje pomoću modernog puta koda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1280">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the modern code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1281">Obuhvaća vrstu rezultata uspješno ili neuspješno metrike performansi spremanja i relevantnih metapodataka dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1281">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1282"> Problemi sa spremanjem mogu uzrokovati gubitak podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1282"> Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1283">Microsoft koristi te podatke da bi osigurao da značajka funkcionira prema očekivanjima i da se korisnički sadržaj uspješno održava.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1283">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsaveas"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1365">Prikuplja se svaki put kada PowerPoint izvodi Spremi u obliku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1365">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a Save As.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1366">Obuhvaća vrstu rezultata uspješno ili neuspješno metrike performansi spremanja i relevantnih metapodataka dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1366">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1367">Problemi sa spremanjem mogu uzrokovati gubitak podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1367">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1368">Microsoft koristi te podatke da bi osigurao da značajka funkcionira prema očekivanjima i da se korisnički sadržaj uspješno održava.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1368">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1369">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long –** neuhvaćene lokalne iznimke dok je aktivnost pokrenuta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long -** Uncaught native exceptions while activity was running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long –** vrijeme tijekom kojeg je aktivnost isključena/nije pokrenuta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long -** Time for which Activity was detached/not running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AssistedReadingReasons:long –** unaprijed definiran skup vrijednosti razloga zbog kojih se dokument otvorio u načinu za pomoć pri čitanju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AssistedReadingReasons:long -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsavelegacy"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1460">Prikuplja se svaki put kada PowerPoint izvodi spremanje pomoću naslijeđenog puta koda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1460">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the legacy code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1461">Obuhvaća vrstu rezultata uspješno ili neuspješno metrike performansi spremanja i relevantnih metapodataka dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1461">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1462">Problemi sa spremanjem mogu uzrokovati gubitak podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1462">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1463">Microsoft koristi te podatke da bi osigurao da značajka funkcionira prema očekivanjima i da se korisnički sadržaj uspješno održava.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1463">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officetranslatortexttranslated"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1740">Office.Translator.TextTranslated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1740">Office.Translator.TextTranslated</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1741">Prikuplja uspjeh ili neuspjeh prijevoda odabira koji korisnik pokreće u servisu Translator SDX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1741">Collects success or failure of a selection translation that a user action triggers in the Translator SDX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1742">To je vrlo važno zbog procjene stanja značajke prijevoda i reagiranja na kvarove koji se mogu dogoditi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1742">This is critical to evaluate the health of the translation feature and react to any outages that might occur.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1743">Koristi se za praćenje stanja scenarija „Prijevod odabira“ u programima Excel, PowerPoint i Word.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1743">Used to monitor the health of the "Translate Selection" scenario in Excel, PowerPoint, Word.</span></span>
