#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccoreautorecoverysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1888">Taj događaj označava da Office Word sprema automatski oporavljeni dokument koji još nije bio spremljen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1888">This event indicates Office Word saves an auto-recovery document that has not been saved before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1889">On Microsoftu omogućuje otkrivanje pogrešaka s automatskim oporavkom, što je važno za zaštitu podataka dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1889">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in auto-recovery which is important for document data safety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1890">Događaj nadzire funkcionira li spremanje automatskog oporavka prema očekivanjima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1890">The event monitors whether auto-recovery-save is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-1891">Koristi se i za izračunavanje broja mjesečnih aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metriku pouzdanosti oblaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1891">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-1892">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-1892">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

### <a name="application-status-and-boot-subtype"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2169">*Podvrsta stanja i pokretanja aplikacije*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2169">*Application status and boot subtype*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2170">Utvrđivanje je li došlo do određenih događaja povezanih sa značajkama, poput pokretanja ili zaustavljanja, te je li značajka pokrenuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2170">Determination if specific feature events have occurred, such as start or stop, and if feature is running.</span></span>

#### <a name="officeextensibilityofficejsappactivated"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2171">Office.Extensibility.OfficeJS.Appactivated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2171">Office.Extensibility.OfficeJS.Appactivated</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationopen"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2396">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Open</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2396">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Open</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2397">Prikuplja se svaki put kada PowerPoint otvori datoteku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2397">Collected whenever PowerPoint opens a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2398">Sadrži informacije o uspješnosti, pojedinosti neuspjeha, metriku performansi i osnovne detalje o datoteci, uključujući vrstu oblika datoteke i metapodatke dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2398">Contains success information, failure details, performance metrics, and basic details about the file including file format type and document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2399">Te su informacije nužne da bi se osiguralo da PowerPoint može uspješno otvarati datoteke bez smanjenja performansi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2399">This information is necessary to ensure PowerPoint can open files successfully with no degradation in performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2400">To omogućuje dijagnosticiranje bilo kakvih problema koje otkrijemo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2400">It allows us to diagnose any problems we discover.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenffileopenxstzcore"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenifrinitargs"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2748">Taj događaj označava da Office Word otvara dokument putem COM aktivacije ili naredbenog retka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2748">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via COM activation or command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2749">Sadrži i ključne podatke o performansama otvaranja datoteka, a iz perspektive korisnika predstavlja događaj pokretanja aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2749">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2750">Događaj nadzire funkcionira li otvaranje datoteka iz naredbenog retka prema očekivanjima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2750">The event monitors whether file-open-from-command-line is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2751">Koristi se i za izračunavanje broja mjesečnih aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metriku pouzdanosti oblaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2751">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2752">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2752">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes –** izvješćuje jesmo li mogli pravilno popuniti ostale vrijednosti vezane uz telemetriju dokumenta u sklopu događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2754">Koristi se za dijagnostiku kvalitete podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2754">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous –** broj (sažetih) bajtova za koje vjerujemo da možemo otvoriti datoteku bez njih ako ih dobijemo prije nego što korisnik poželi početi uređivati ili možda spremati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork –** broj (sažetih) bajtova bez kojih bismo možda mogli otvoriti datoteku, ali bi to zahtijevalo značajna ulaganja u kod</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous –** broj (sažetih) bajtova koje moramo imati prije nego što možemo početi otvarati datoteku</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown –** broj bajtova u dijelovima dokumenta koje ne očekujemo pronaći.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode –** dokument je samo za čitanje ili za uređivanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenloadfile"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2813">Taj događaj označava da Office Word otvara dokument putem dijaloškog okvira Otvaranje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2813">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via Open dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2814">Sadrži i ključne podatke o performansama otvaranja datoteka, a iz perspektive korisnika predstavlja događaj pokretanja aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2814">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2815">Događaj nadzire funkcionira li otvaranje datoteke putem dijaloškog okvira Otvaranje prema očekivanjima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2815">The event monitors whether file-open-from-the-open-file-dialog is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2816">Koristi se i za izračunavanje broja mjesečnih aktivnih korisnika/uređaja i metriku pouzdanosti oblaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2816">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2817">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2817">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes –** izvješćuje jesmo li mogli pravilno popuniti ostale vrijednosti vezane uz telemetriju dokumenta u sklopu događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2819">Koristi se za dijagnostiku kvalitete podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2819">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous –** broj (sažetih) bajtova za koje vjerujemo da možemo otvoriti datoteku bez njih ako ih dobijemo prije nego što korisnik poželi početi uređivati ili možda spremati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous –** broj (sažetih) bajtova koje moramo imati prije nego što možemo početi otvarati datoteku</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="65b74-2824">**Data\_DetachedDuration –** koliko je dugo aktivnost bila odvojena od niti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2824">**Data\_DetachedDuration -** How long was the activity detached from the thread</span></span>

## <a name="product-and-service-performance-data-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-2910">Događaji koji se odnose na podatke o performansama proizvoda i usluga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2910">Product and service performance data events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2911">Ovo su podvrste podataka u toj kategoriji:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2911">The following are the data subtypes in this category:</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2912">Neočekivano zatvaranje (rušenje) aplikacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2912">Unexpected application exit (crash)</span></span>](#unexpected-application-exit-crash-subtype)
- [<span data-ttu-id="65b74-2913">Performanse značajki aplikacije </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-2913">Application feature performance </span></span>](#application-feature-performance-subtype)

### <a name="application-activity-error-subtype"></a><span data-ttu-id="65b74-3175">*Podvrsta pogreške aktivnosti aplikacije*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="65b74-3175">*Application activity error subtype*</span></span>
